# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes CNI Network Plugin Interface Architecture

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the CNI (Container Network Interface) integration: the CNI plugin invocation, the network namespace setup, the IP address management (IPAM) call, and the network plugin manager that coordinates CNI calls during pod creation.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

78-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've created a comprehensive analysis of the CNI (Container Network Interface) integration in kubernetes/kubernetes (v1.32.0). Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

I've identified **10 key Go source files** that implement CNI integration in Kubernetes:

### Key Files:
1. **`pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go`** - Pod sandbox creation (network namespace setup)
2. **`pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go`** - Network operations and pod CIDR updates
3. **`pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go`** - Pod creation orchestration
4. **`pkg/kubelet/kubelet.go`** - Main pod sync entry point
5. **`staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/`** - CRI (Container Runtime Interface) definitions
6. **`staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go`** - CRI runtime client
7. **`pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/range_allocator.go`** - Cluster-level IPAM

### Key Functions in Call Chain:
1. `SyncPod()` - Pod lifecycle orchestration
2. `createPodSandbox()` - Network namespace setup
3. `generatePodSandboxConfig()` - Network configuration generation
4. `NetworkNamespaceForPod()` - Network namespace mode determination
5. `updatePodCIDR()` - Pod CIDR routing updates
6. `RunPodSandbox()` - CRI interface for pod sandbox creation

The analysis reveals that **Kubernetes v1.32.0 delegates actual CNI plugin invocation to the CRI runtime** (containerd/CRI-O), while Kubernetes itself manages the orchestration, CIDR allocation, and configuration generation. This separation of concerns allows Kubernetes to remain agnostic to specific network plugins.

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json`.

Architecture in Kubernetes v1.32.0\\n\\n### Overview\\nKubernetes v1.32.0 implements CNI (Container Network Interface) integration through a delegation model where the Container Runtime Interface (CRI) handles the actual CNI plugin invocation. The kubelet orchestrates the network setup lifecycle by:\\n\\n1. **Pod Sandbox Creation** - Initiating network namespace setup\\n2. **Network IP Assignment** - Waiting for and retrieving pod network IPs\\n3. **Pod CIDR Management** - Updating cluster-level CIDR routing\\n\\n### Key Components\\n\\n#### 1. Network Setup Entry Point\\n**File**: `pkg/kubelet/kubelet.go` - `SyncPod()` function\\n- Main orchestration function called during pod lifecycle\\n- Checks network readiness before proceeding with pod creation\\n- Delegates to kuberuntime for actual pod creation\\n\\n#### 2. Pod Sandbox Creation (Network Namespace Setup)\\n**Files**:\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go` - Contains `kubeGenericRuntimeManager` that coordinates pod creation\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go` - Implements `createPodSandbox()` function\\n  - Calls `generatePodSandboxConfig()` to prepare network configuration\\n  - Invokes `m.runtimeService.RunPodSandbox()` which delegates to CRI runtime\\n  - The CRI runtime (containerd/CRI-O) calls CNI plugins to set up network namespaces\\n  - Returns pod sandbox ID with assigned IP address\\n\\n**Key Function**: `createPodSandbox()` at line 39\\n- Generates pod sandbox configuration with network settings\\n- Calls CRI RuntimeService.RunPodSandbox\\n- The CRI implementation handles actual CNI plugin invocation\\n\\n#### 3. Network Configuration Generation\\n**File**: `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go` - `generatePodSandboxConfig()`\\n- Gets DNS configuration via `GetPodDNS()` from RuntimeHelper\\n- Sets up network namespace mode (POD or NODE) via `NetworkNamespaceForPod()`\\n- Configures Linux-specific network options\\n- Passes configuration to CRI runtime\\n\\n#### 4. Network Namespace Management\\n**File**: `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/util/util.go` - `NetworkNamespaceForPod()`\\n- Determines network namespace mode for pod\\n- Returns `NODE` for host-networked pods\\n- Returns `POD` for regular pods requiring CNI setup\\n\\n#### 5. Pod CIDR and IPAM Management\\n**Files**:\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go` - Network-related kubelet operations\\n  - `updatePodCIDR()` - Updates cluster pod CIDR routing information\\n  - `GetPodDNS()` - Retrieves DNS configuration for pods\\n- `pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/range_allocator.go` - IPAM allocation for cluster nodes\\n  - `AllocateOrOccupyCIDR()` - Allocates CIDR ranges to nodes\\n  - `ReleaseNodeCIDR()` - Releases CIDR ranges\\n\\n#### 6. CRI Runtime Interface Definitions\\n**Files**:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto` - Protocol buffer definitions\\n  - `RunPodSandboxRequest` - Configuration for pod sandbox creation\\n  - `RunPodSandboxResponse` - Returns pod sandbox ID and network status\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go` - Interface definitions\\n  - `PodSandboxManager` interface - Defines pod sandbox operations\\n  - `RuntimeService` interface - Main CRI service interface\\n\\n#### 7. CRI Runtime Client Implementation\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go`\\n- `remoteRuntimeService` - gRPC implementation of RuntimeService\\n- `RunPodSandbox()` - Calls CRI runtime's RunPodSandbox method\\n- Handles communication with containerd/CRI-O daemons\\n\\n#### 8. Runtime Helper Interface\\n**File**: `pkg/kubelet/container/helpers.go` - `RuntimeHelper` interface\\n- `GenerateRunContainerOptions()` - Generates container runtime options including network settings\\n- `GetPodDNS()` - Retrieves DNS configuration\\n- `GetPodCgroupParent()` - Gets cgroup configuration\\n- Methods for resource management and pod configuration\\n\\n### Network Setup Call Chain\\n\\n1. `kubelet.SyncPod()` (pkg/kubelet/kubelet.go)\\n   - Checks network plugin readiness\\n   - Calls kuberuntime manager to create pod\\n\\n2. `kubeGenericRuntimeManager.createPodSandbox()` (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go)\\n   - Coordinates pod sandbox creation\\n\\n3. `createPodSandbox()` (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go)\\n   - Generates pod sandbox config via `generatePodSandboxConfig()`\\n   - Calls `runtimeService.RunPodSandbox(config, runtimeHandler)`\\n\\n4. `remoteRuntimeService.RunPodSandbox()` (staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go)\\n   - Makes gRPC call to CRI runtime (containerd/CRI-O)\\n   - Passes PodSandboxConfig with network settings\\n\\n5. **CRI Runtime** (external - containerd/CRI-O)\\n   - Receives RunPodSandboxRequest\\n   - Creates network namespace\\n   - **Invokes CNI plugins** (e.g., bridge, flannel, calico)\\n   - Assigns IP address via CNI IPAM plugins\\n   - Returns pod sandbox ID with network status (IP address)\\n\\n6. `kubelet.updatePodCIDR()` (pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go)\\n   - Updates runtime state with pod CIDR\\n   - Calls `runtimeService.UpdatePodCIDR()` for cluster networking\\n\\n### IPAM (IP Address Management)\\n\\nIPAM implementation spans two levels:\\n\\n1. **Cluster-level IPAM** (pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/)\\n   - Allocates Pod CIDR ranges to nodes\\n   - `RangeAllocator` manages cluster-wide CIDR allocation\\n   - Communicates ranges to kubelet via node.Spec.PodCIDRs\\n\\n2. **Pod-level IPAM** (delegated to CRI)\\n   - CRI runtime calls CNI IPAM plugins\\n   - IPAM plugins assign specific IPs to pods from node CIDR ranges\\n   - Returns assigned IP to kubelet\\n\\n### Summary\\n\\nThe CNI integration in Kubernetes v1.32.0 follows a clear delegation model:\\n- **Kubernetes** handles: Pod lifecycle management, network readiness checks, CIDR allocation and routing, pod configuration generation\\n- **CRI Runtime** handles: Network namespace creation, CNI plugin invocation, pod-level IPAM\\n\\nThis separation of concerns allows Kubernetes to remain agnostic to specific network plugins while the CRI runtime manages the actual network setup through standardized CNI plugins.\"\n}\nEOF\ncat /workspace/answer.json\n"

Runtime Helper Interface\n**File**: `pkg/kubelet/container/helpers.go` - `RuntimeHelper` interface\n- `GenerateRunContainerOptions()` - Generates container runtime options including network settings\n- `GetPodDNS()` - Retrieves DNS configuration\n- `GetPodCgroupParent()` - Gets cgroup configuration\n- Methods for resource management and pod configuration\n\n### Network Setup Call Chain\n\n1. `kubelet.SyncPod()` (pkg/kubelet/kubelet.go)\n   - Checks network plugin readiness\n   - Calls kuberuntime manager to create pod\n\n2. `kubeGenericRuntimeManager.createPodSandbox()` (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go)\n   - Coordinates pod sandbox creation\n\n3. `createPodSandbox()` (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go)\n   - Generates pod sandbox config via `generatePodSandboxConfig()`\n   - Calls `runtimeService.RunPodSandbox(config, runtimeHandler)`\n\n4. `remoteRuntimeService.RunPodSandbox()` (staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go)\n   - Makes gRPC call to CRI runtime (containerd/CRI-O)\n   - Passes PodSandboxConfig with network settings\n\n5. **CRI Runtime** (external - containerd/CRI-O)\n   - Receives RunPodSandboxRequest\n   - Creates network namespace\n   - **Invokes CNI plugins** (e.g., bridge, flannel, calico)\n   - Assigns IP address via CNI IPAM plugins\n   - Returns pod sandbox ID with network status (IP address)\n\n6. `kubelet.updatePodCIDR()` (pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go)\n   - Updates runtime state with pod CIDR\n   - Calls `runtimeService.UpdatePodCIDR()` for cluster networking\n\n### IPAM (IP Address Management)\n\nIPAM implementation spans two levels:\n\n1. **Cluster-level IPAM** (pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/)\n   - Allocates Pod CIDR ranges to nodes\n   - `RangeAllocator` manages cluster-wide CIDR allocation\n   - Communicates ranges to kubelet via node.Spec.PodCIDRs\n\n2. **Pod-level IPAM** (delegated to CRI)\n   - CRI runtime calls CNI IPAM plugins\n   - IPAM plugins assign specific IPs to pods from node CIDR ranges\n   - Returns assigned IP to kubelet\n\n### Summary\n\nThe CNI integration in Kubernetes v1.32.0 follows a clear delegation model:\n- **Kubernetes** handles: Pod lifecycle management, network readiness checks, CIDR allocation and routing, pod configuration generation\n- **CRI Runtime** handles: Network namespace creation, CNI plugin invocation, pod-level IPAM\n\nThis separation of concerns allows Kubernetes to remain agnostic to specific network plugins while the CRI runtime manages the actual network setup through standardized CNI plugins."
}
